 454 11 farvari ko banaras main rahul gandhi or akhilesh yadav ke road sho kii khabar kai dinon se aa rahi thi
 For this, the people of the Congress Party were also busy preparing
 root bhi tay kar liya gaya tha or espiji ke logon kii bhi shahar main aane kii khabar sthaneey akhbaar main pramukhataa se chap rahi thi
 But late Thursday night, when the news of this roadshow not coming came, it became a matter of discussion
 congress ke logon ne bataaya ki chunki buddha poornima ke din sant ravidaas kii jayanti hoti he or badi sankhya main unke anuyaayi yahaan aate hai, lihaaja us bheed ko dekhte hue is road sho ko cancel kiya gaya he
 The comments gauratlab he ki 11 taarikh ko hi pehle charan kaa matdaan he
 According to sources, the way Modi's road show took place in Benaras on the day of first phase of Lok Sabha elections and its impact was also visible
 thik usee tarj par is road sho ko prashanth kishor ne tay kiya tha lekin akhilesh ke 11 taarikh ke liye pehle se hi kaarykram tay the
 Therefore, the program of both of them was not being made jointly
 isi vajah se 3 din se espiji banaras kii taiyaari dekh rahi thi, iske baavjood bhi aadhikarik kaarykram nahin ban paaya tha
 District Magistrate of Benares Yogeshwar Ram Mishra also says that no protocol had come to CM Akhilesh's arrival
 isaliye is kaarykram ke hone kii unhen koi jaankaree nahin thi
 In fact, with this shared rally in Banaras after sp-congress alliance, both parties want to give a big message
 yah road sho isliye bhi ahm he kyonki banaras piem modi kaa garh mana jaataa he
 In such a situation, the sp-congress wants Rahul and Akhilesh to start a common rally instead of alone
 aise main is vakt akhilesh ke banaras na aa paane ki sthiti main congress ne ravidaas jayanti kii aad lete hue kah diya ki bheed kii vajah se road sho ko radd kar diya gaya he
 Congressmen say that now this road show can be done any day after the last date of nomination of 16th
 vaise banaras main piem modi kii raily 3 march ko pehle se prastaavit he
 Elections in Benares and its adjoining district are to be held in the final phase on the 8th

 darasal sapa-congress gathbandhan ke baad banaras main is saajha raily ke saath donon hi partiyaan ek bada sandesh dena chaahati hai
 This road show is also important because Banaras is considered to be the stronghold of PM Modi

 america or siie kaa bhi naam aata he

 iske paas hathiyaar or dhan kahaan se aa rahaa he

 sanders ne kaha he ki iraq hamale kii garbh se hi alqaida or ISIS kaa janm hua he

 hillari clinton ne kaha ki ISIS kaa prasar internet ke kaaran ho rahaa he

 galati america kii thi to ab hillari clinton kyon kah rahi hai ki yah sirf america kii ladaai nahin he
